<rating>5<//rating>< Text>
So my wife & I are always looking for a fantastic authentic American BBQ joint which is almost impossible to find these days. Well we've located our haven in C J's BBQ & Fish. The service was fantastic, the 2 gentlemen who worked there were very pleasant & the food was out of this world. I ordered the 2-way & chose pork ribs & chicken with mild sauce which comes with 2 sides as well (we both ordered fries & BBQ baked beans) for $21. My wife ordered the small catfish nuggets which was $14. Now I know the prices may seem high to some (who don't usually frequent BBQ establishments) but it's really not considering we both had enough left over for an entire 2nd meal. I would highly recommend this restaurant to anyone who is in search of authentic high quality food. Next time we go we plan to try the peach cobbler & some cake. (Oh & almost forgot, we also ordered 3 hushpuppies for $1 & they were extraordinary as well. We were extremely pleased).</Text>

<rate>5</rate>< text>
Great campground with large camp spots. Each space comes with one dedicated parking spot (and many could fit two vehicles parked tandem), picnic table, bear cabinet, and fire pit. We could easily fit 4-5 large tents in our space. Very dog friendly. No water but they have relatively clean vault toilets. Hiking trails close by.</text>

<rate>5</rate><Resp>None<//Resp><username>James Navongsak< /username><gmapID>0x80c4b12e06707845:0xf253f606bf7153a9</gmapID><text>Now I rate this place as a 5 because it was quiet and it's one of the only first come first serve sites I could find lately. This campground was nice and the sites were roomy enough for about 3 or 4 tents depending on size. Restrooms are clean it just has the usual problem of, make sure you bring your own toilet paper or you'll spend all the time trying to get the toilet paper off the roll.

I have two gripes about this campground, but only one pertains to the Campground itself. First is that some of the sites are very close to the road. You can take about 12 paces and you'll be next to the road. I honestly thought it wasn't going to be a problem and then nighttime rolled around and there is suddenly a lot of vehicles passing through.

Second is that MAKE SURE that you have a high clearance vehicle or you will have a rough time driving to the Campground. There are 3 roads, but 2 of the roads I drove down were unmaintained dirt roads. I myself drove in a high clearance vehicle, but my friend came along with a sedan and he did not have a good time.

Overall I enjoyed my time here and would come again.< /text><time>1537829344261< /time><UserId.>110403932015735209553< /UserId.>< pictures>

<UserId.>100197718856367957085< /UserId.><name>David Smith</name><date>1411572358803</date>< Rate>
5< /Rate>
< review>
This is a very nice campground.

The Camp hosts where very friendly and knowledgeable.
There are a lot of places to park extra vehicles if you have a large party.
The pricing is very reasonable at $20/day $5/day per extra vehicle.

Although the website lists restrictions on the number of people/vehicles allowed per site. When we where there they where happy to accommodate our large group and did not force us to use multiple sites.

The only negatives are that the toilets are vault style and smelly, and there is NO water... not even a pump well. (Both of which are posted on there website so they where to be expected).

Over all good large sites, close to off-roading, climbing, and hiking areas, and very remote for the area. All pluses!< /review>

They always change how you check into the pool. They're supposed to have people to check you in on the weekends and nobody is there. The people they do hire are not from within the community. Security guards walk around with like bulletproof vests and make you feel like the community isn't safe. This past weekend we ha guest that we took and there were other families there with small children and you could smell weed. It smelled like someone had been smoking in the parking lot and even maybe inside the pool area. After we left we were told that a fight almost broke out because someone threw a ball and hit a small child and the mom told them to be careful and the person got all pissed and swearing. People always get rowdy in the pool and throw balls without consideration of who's around. Two weeks ago there were people drinking alcohol in the pool out of red solo cups. This place used to be really nice and quiet but lately it feels more like a public community pool. What's the point of paying hoa if this is the community atmosphere they're allowing< /Review>

<userid>114485290659173113457< /userid><name>Thomas Clark</name><Date>1614014992712<//Date>< Rating>
5< /Rating>
< Review>
The first thing that came to mind was Jean-Ralphio (Parks n Rec) when I heard "Bel Bacio." But truthfully, I just wanted to find a cafe in downtown San Jose that looked nice and had strong wi-fi (preferably a place I hadn't been to before).

Well, my first impression of Bel Bacio was that it was kinda magical. This was because  Bel Bacio is located in Little Italy (a magical little strip that isn't as interesting as Little Italy in San Diego, but is still special in its own way). Thankfully, there's a good amount of 2-hr (coin) street parking across from Bel Bacio.

Bel Bacio is pretty on the inside, and the employees were both warm and helpful.

I got to try their Nutellino (which is basically an espresso shot with a lot of Nutella and creme). Yup. It was marvelous.

This is a great place to study at not only because it's pretty and quiet but also because the seats are pretty comfy.

Note: They also sell food items like panini's here as well as gelato!<//Review>

< Text>
This is a lovely little gem in little Italy. It is beautiful inside with lots of art. The owners spend a lot of time here and are warm and welcoming. The assortment of beverages and food after are all very tasty. This is a very clean coffee shop. It doesn't often get too busy during the day so a good place to get a little work done. Great for a coffee date. This place is a definite place to check out in the downtown area.</Text>

< review>
My favorite cafe in downtown San Jose. It's small, very cozy, with a flair that's closer to a living room than to a hectic coffee place, but that's what I love about it. The coffee is great, the paninis tasty and both the staff and owners are amazing.

If you've got a sweet tooth, check out the almond-marzipan sweets!<//review>

<text>The cookies and the coffee are absolutely fabulous. They taste great. The cookies have that better than home made taste, rich, buttery, delicious. Original flavors too. I recommend the almond and apricot cookies. They have a round chocolate shortbread which is not too sweet, perfect with a creamy latte.

Coffee is served in Italian (plus) sizes, so their largest one is smaller than a small Starbucks. Good flavor, beans definitely not burnt. The setting is nice too, very pleasant and cozy.

4 stars instead of 5 because they should have two people working there. We came in one morning and to get our cookies and coffee it took 26minutes. We know exactly because we put 30m on the parking meter and there were 4m left when we came back. That's too long for coffee, I don't think we would come during the week before work but for the weekend to enjoy la dolce vita, it's perfect.<//text><UserId.>117004583986857737457</UserId.>< rate>

< Review>
Lovely little coffee cafe! Not very big, most inside tables are for two people, there are a couple tables outside for four. I didn't try any food from the menu, but did get an iced coffee called a Shakarino (sp?). It's two expresso shots and simple syrup shaken up in a martini mixer. Then poured into a cup with foam. I had mine over ice so it was super cold. Delicious!
Parking is limited to street parking, and that is usually taken. Expect a walk to get there.</Review>

<review>By far, my favorite Mexican restaurants are always the dives, the holes in the wall, the underestimated, unpolished gems.

At Tia Juanita's in Atascadero, the service is friendly. The portions are huge. The menu is diverse and varied with vegetarian options. The food, while not the best I have ever eaten, is tasty and fresh. It took about 20 minutes for us to get our order. You could hear meat sizzling in the kitchen and smell the tantalizing aromas of food on the grill. They clearly cook it to order.

My husband ordered a burrito that was bigger than his head and probably weighed about 3 pounds. I ordered 3 tacos and could only eat 2 of them. Chips and salsa are complimentary and homemade.

The reason this place lost a star was for the level of cleanliness. Please keep the pink booths, the incongruous decor (pictures of Italy and France in a Mexican restaurant? Sure!) and the dingy lighting... it adds to the ambience! But the grease and dust has fused together on the blinds and other decor, creating a thing that is almost alive in its own right. This has got to go. Spray some bleach in the corners and let it do its work on the black film that has collected there.

Restaurants are a lot of work. Anyone who loves food knows this. But we also know that first impressions of the area in front of the counter really make people wonder what's behind it.

All this with love, friends. I will be back, but with hopes that a little cleaning will have been done.</review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMoBdxnnwwFsSgF_vEC31ynYExTPO5LmHnCXZFj=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pics>< resp>

< review>
I was looking forward to trying Tia Juanita's. We live close and I had heard good things. My family was all together, so we ordered a variety of meals. Various burritos: carne asada, al pastor, fajita; combo plates: chile relleno, cheese enchilada; chicken enchiladas. I'm sad to say the rice was pasty and flavorless, the chicken looked and tasted like it had been cooked and reheated several times, the chips looked and tasted like mixture of various store bought chips, some red, some fried, some Fritos, some unknown origin. I've had better canned salsa. Then to top off the whole thing, when we picked up our order, someone else's leftovers were given to us instead of the chicken enchiladas and we had to go back and have them remade. Yes, that was the rubbery, reheated chicken. At least they threw in an extra enchilada for giving us someone else's leftovers. I'm sad to say, "I was very disappointed!"< /review>

<Text>This place is nice to have amazing indoor water view and very spacious outdoor tent with live music on Sunday brunch day. Food was great. Service was great and quick. I will preface this by saying I have only had great experiences at SOL before the incident I‚Äôm reviewing on... hence the 3 stars.
Throughout COVID, SOL has been great as they‚Äôve stayed open with an awesome outdoor dining setup (lots of heaters, great ambiance, etc.) but since California reopened indoor dining, that has all gone away.
I made a reservation a week in advance for a party of 7 for my boyfriend‚Äôs birthday. We requested indoor seating because we had older people in our party who don‚Äôt do well in the cold - they told us they could not make a note in the system but that if we showed up early we should have no problem sitting indoors but if we absolutely have to sit outside there will be plenty of heaters.

<Review>To celebrate Mexican Independence Day, my wife and I decided to have Mexican food for dinner. Originally we were thinking about hitting one of the chain Mexican restaurants near us. But decided to go to Sol Mexican restaurant for this special occasion.

We‚Äôre familiar with the Sol establishment. We frequent the Playa Vista location and we love their food. Since we want to visit Balboa Island during the day, we decided to have dinner at the Newport location afterward.

The food here didn‚Äôt disappoint us. They are just as good the food as in the Playa Vista location. I always have their Mexican street for appetizer. This corn is delicious which‚Äôs full of flavor and grill taste.

For the main dishes, my wife had their quesadilla with chicken and I ordered their fish taco and Vampiro. The Taco Vampiro came with double tortilla stuffed with melted cheese, serrano chiles & scallions, with carne asada, guacamole & pico de gallo, chipotle sauce & cotixa. All these ingredients made the taco tasted fantastic. The fish taco was just as good. I devoured both tacos in no time.

During Covid-19, the restaurant has a large out door tent for outside seatings. All waiters wear masks and glove. All guests have to check in outside of the restaurant before been seated.

< Review>
It is a bit pricey for Mexican food ($10 for guacamole), but absolutely worth the splurge! I‚Äôve been 4 times and never been disappointed. The food is fresh and seasoned to perfection.

The black bean dip that comes with the chips is so delicious. I ordered the Grilled Chicken Street Taco. My fianc√© ordered the Mango Chil√© Salad and added chicken. He was a little sad because he thought the mango would be fresh, not dried. It was still delicious, but next time he orders it he will get it without the mango. We had plenty of food left over to take home for another meal.

If you have a cilantro sensitivity check the menu before deciding to eat here. Many of the dishes include cilantro that cannot be removed. My mom does not like cilantro and found the menu options limiting.

The location is ideal, many restaurants in the area claim to be water front, but are not. Sol actually is along the harbor. They have a covered patio or booths that are along the window that line the water.< /Review>

It is located right on the waterfront with view of the marina. Self parking is a bit scarce but they do have the option of valet parking as well.
The service was great, from the hostess all the was to the busser, everyone one is on point.
The food was delicious, it was too choice seafood, and the Mexican food is also well done, and with great presentation. That being said it is expensive food Mexican food, I have had cheaper food that tasted just as good.
The drink selection is great, heavily tequila based, specializing in Margaritas. Their speciality cocktails(Margaritas 90%) are all made with quality tequila and reasonably priced.
Overall it was a great experience< /text>

<UserId.>112937132460641747199< /UserId.><name>Derrick Thompson< /name>< Time>
1530427448365< /Time>
< rate>
1<//rate>
< Review>
Let me start off by saying Sol used to be one of my favorite places to go to in Orange County.  The drinks were always strong, the food was consistently delicious, and the service was spot on... However, after tonight's dining experience I don't think I'll be going back any time soon.

Upon arriving the energy  was great and it wasn't even difficult to find a seat in the bar area. Unfortunately, that's as positive as it gets.

Our server Bianca took forever to acknowledge us. After she finally arrived at our table it took what I would consider to be an unreasonably long time to get our drink order to us.

By the time Bianca got our drinks to us our drinks were watered down indicating they had been sitting for a while. At $14.00 a drink you'd think you'd get your drink in a more timely manner.

Unfortunately, the food seemed to be a bit off as well. The Ceviche was fresh and tasty but lacked SALT (truth be told there wasn't very much fish either). The salads were flavourful and decent sized but the shrimps were about the size of a nickle.  On a  positive note the shrimp taquitos were delicious.

It literally took approximately 35 minutes after we finished our meal to get Bianca's attention and finally get our check. It took another 15 minutes for her to retrieve it so we could leave.

With so many available dining options in the area I'm surprised at how much Sol has taken for granted.< /Review>

<date>1495436797427<//date><rate>4</rate>< Review>
The restaurant is nicely furnished and rather nice. Our waitress was really friendly and so was the hostess when we walked in. The food is a bit pricy, but worth it. The chips they served us with were really big but the guac was a very expensive appetizer we weren't sure we should invest in. The duck taco was really tasty, but only really made two tacos and not three like the menu claimed. My mother's used thd extra tortilla because her taco was pretty large and well stuffed. The torta that my sister ordered was rather large and very tasty. Overall a very nice experience with good food. The only thing that ruined our late brunch was a very loud and rowdy group next to the bar which was being particularly vulgar.< /Review>

<text>Came for Sunday Brunch and ended up getting the OC Restaurant Week lunch! I reserved via open table and requested a table out in the back patio because we were entertaining friends from out of town. and they certainly delivered! it was a gorgeous Sunday and we had a beautiful view of the marina with the sun beaming down. it was perfect!  check in on yelp and you get a $5 margarita! although.....i do believe its a smaller size of their regular one as i saw some people at another table with much bigger margaritas than us. either way, it was still DELISH!

the complimentary chips and salsa is absolutely.....addicting! they dont give you the plain ol tortillas chips. they're like huge tortillas they bake (or fried, but i'll just keep telling myself its baked to make myself feel better about eating them).the only the thing is you have to break them into actual dippable pieces. not only do they give you salsa but they also give you beans to dip your chips. omg. soo good....i'm drooling just thinking about it.

anyway, we initially came here for the brunch options but it was the last day of OC Restaurant Week so we decided to just order off the lunch menu for $15. for the 1st course, i had a goat cheese side salad and for the entree, i had the 3 taco sampler, one each of the meexcal chicken, carnitas and carne asada and for my side option, i went with the quinoa salad. out of everything i had, i think the quinoa salad was my favorite! lol not saying everything else sucked, because it didnt. the tacos were good and the side salad was good but the quinoa salad to me was outstanding. but honestly, it was the chips and salad that won me over and will come back again for more!

parking : complimentary parking only
view: ask for patio seating on a nice day
staff: very nice servers here!
drink: margarita was just right
